                <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/03/i-rotated-a-beginner-pattern-and-it-turned-intermediate" title="I Rotated a Beginner Pattern… and It Turned Intermediate">I Rotated a Beginner Pattern… and It Turned Intermediate</a></h3>

                <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/built-from-the-middle-out-randomized-bracelet-with-intentional-chaos" title="Built from the Middle Out?! Randomized Bracelet with Intentional Chaos">Built from the Middle Out?! Randomized Bracelet with Intentional Chaos</a></h3>
                
                <div class="entry-summary">
          <p>Today we’re upping the chaos—but also the control. This new freestyle bracelet starts in the center, not the top, allowing for a huge central diamond and full symmetry in two directions. It’s part of my ongoing experiment into randomized pattern design, inspired by South American&nbsp;<a class="read-more" href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/built-from-the-middle-out-randomized-bracelet-with-intentional-chaos">&hellip;</a></p>

                <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/the-most-chaotic-bracelet-ive-ever-designed-random-symmetry-challenge" title="The Most Chaotic Bracelet I’ve Ever Designed? | Random Symmetry Challenge">The Most Chaotic Bracelet I’ve Ever Designed? | Random Symmetry Challenge</a></h3>

This pattern uses 24 single strands, 4 colors, and absolutely no chill. 😂 Inspired by a Reddit user asking, “Can someone make a pattern out of randomness?” I decided to try.                 <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/freestyling-a-2-color-bracelet-pattern-12-strings-will-it-work" title="Freestyling a 2-Color Bracelet Pattern (12 Strings!) – Will It Work?">Freestyling a 2-Color Bracelet Pattern (12 Strings!) – Will It Work?</a></h3>
                
                <div class="entry-summary">
          <p>What happens when you have a cool idea for a bracelet… and just wing it? 🎯 In this video, I freestyle a brand-new two-color pattern using 12 strings (the same color combo from my 10-string kumi video 👀). The idea? Elongated diamonds stacked in threes,&nbsp;<a class="read-more" href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/freestyling-a-2-color-bracelet-pattern-12-strings-will-it-work">&hellip;</a></p>

                <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/decoding-a-lost-bracelet-pattern" title="Decoding a Lost Bracelet Pattern">Decoding a Lost Bracelet Pattern</a></h3>
                
                <div class="entry-summary">
          <p>I was handed a bracelet fragment and asked to figure out the original pattern—no notes, no diagram, just knots and guesswork. 😅 Challenge accepted. In this video, I walk through my process of reverse engineering the pattern knot by knot. It’s a bit weird, definitely&nbsp;<a class="read-more" href="https://akaawol.com/2026/02/decoding-a-lost-bracelet-pattern">&hellip;</a></p>

                <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/01/can-my-custom-arrowhead-pattern-work-with-just-12-strings-lets-find-out" title="Can My Custom Arrowhead Pattern Work with Just 12 Strings?                 <h3 class="entry-title"><a href="https://akaawol.com/2026/01/designing-a-new-elongated-arrowhead-bracelet" title="Designing a New Elongated Arrowhead Bracelet">Designing a New Elongated Arrowhead Bracelet</a></h3>
                
                <div class="entry-summary">
          <p>Hey everyone, it’s Kevin (aka AWOL), and today I’m designing a brand-new arrowhead-style bracelet pattern—but with a twist: instead of stopping at one diamond, this one stacks multiple diamonds in a row, stretching the design and changing the entire rhythm. 🌀 What makes it different?&nbsp;<a class="read-more" href="https://akaawol.com/2026/01/designing-a-new-elongated-arrowhead-bracelet">&hellip;</a></p>
